<div class="mw-parser-output"><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 300px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/aesthetics/images/3/34/Rococo%2C_Urbancore_and_Minimalist_comparison.png/revision/latest?cb=20230730224832" class="image"><img alt="Rococo, Urbancore and Minimalist comparison" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/aesthetics/images/3/34/Rococo%2C_Urbancore_and_Minimalist_comparison.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20230730224832" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="300" height="533" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rococo, Urbancore and Minimalist comparison.png" data-image-key="Rococo%2C_Urbancore_and_Minimalist_comparison.png" data-relevant="1" /></a> 	 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rococo,_Urbancore_and_Minimalist_comparison.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Aesthetics and styles are not limited only to fashion. They have also manifestations in music, architecture, furniture, ceramic, graphic design, interior design, illustration, painting, sculpture and art in general. Here, each row of two pictures shows how <a href="/wiki/Rococo" title="Rococo">Rococo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Urbancore" title="Urbancore">Urbancore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Minimalism" title="Minimalism">Minimalism</a> are manifested through multiple media. The first picture of each row shows an outfit that encapsulates that aesthetic, and the second is with something else that belongs there</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/aesthetics/images/d/dd/Aesthetics_mosaic.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230724003105" class="image"><img alt="Aesthetics mosaic" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/aesthetics/images/d/dd/Aesthetics_mosaic.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230724003105" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="180" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Aesthetics mosaic.jpg" data-image-key="Aesthetics_mosaic.jpg" data-relevant="1" /></a> 	 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Aesthetics_mosaic.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Alphabetically ordered mosaic of almost all aesthetics (as of July 2023)</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>If you need assistance with identifying your aesthetic or creating a moodboard, feel free to ask questions in the <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener" class="text" href="https://aesthetics.fandom.com/f">Discussion Tab</a> (in the pull-down bar of the "Explore" tab at the top of the page), the official <a target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener" class="external text" href="https://discord.com/invite/AQedRGj">Aesthetics Discord Server</a>, or on the <a target="_blank" rel="nofollow noreferrer noopener" class="external text" href="https://www.reddit.com/r/aesthetics/">Aesthetics Subreddit</a>.  
</p>
